Ever heard of resting heart rate?

It’s not just a number - it’s a window into your heart’s efficiency.

Why should you care? Because a lower resting heart rate often means a stronger, more efficient heart. It’s like upgrading from a leaky faucet to a power washer - one strong beat, and boom! Job done. 💥

But here’s where it gets interesting: our healthcare system often overlooks this crucial indicator. Instead of focusing on strengthening your heart, they’re quick to manage symptoms. It’s like putting a band-aid on a leaky pipe instead of fixing the plumbing. 🚰

The good news?

You don’t need to be an Olympian to improve your heart health. Regular aerobic exercise doesn’t just strengthen your heart - it fortifies your entire cardiovascular system. It’s a full-body upgrade, not just a quick fix. 🏃‍♀️🚴‍♂️🏊‍♂️

So, here’s my challenge to you: Check your resting heart rate today. Then, commit to just 15 minutes of cardio daily for a month. Track the change. You might be surprised at what your heart can do when you give it a chance. 📊

Personally, my resting heart rate is 39 beats per minute.

Drop your starting resting heart rate below 👇

Ever heard of resting heart rate?

It’s not just a number - it’s a window into your heart’s efficiency.

Why should you care? Because a lower resting heart rate often means a stronger, more efficient heart. It’s like upgrading from a leaky faucet to a power washer - one strong beat, and boom! Job done. 💥

But here’s where it gets interesting: our healthcare system often overlooks this crucial indicator. Instead of focusing on strengthening your heart, they’re quick to manage symptoms. It’s like putting a band-aid on a leaky pipe instead of fixing the plumbing. 🚰

The good news?

You don’t need to be an Olympian to improve your heart health. Regular aerobic exercise doesn’t just strengthen your heart - it fortifies your entire cardiovascular system. It’s a full-body upgrade, not just a quick fix. 🏃‍♀️🚴‍♂️🏊‍♂️

So, here’s my challenge to you: Check your resting heart rate today. Then, commit to just 15 minutes of cardio daily for a month. Track the change. You might be surprised at what your heart can do when you give it a chance. 📊

Personally, my resting heart rate is 39 beats per minute.

Drop your starting resting heart rate below 👇
